--- Model Psychometrics Analysis ---

Model: stabilityai/StableBeluga-7B
  - Average WLI for 'dense' prompts (Mean Depth): 16.3012
  - Average WLI for 'flat' prompts (Mean Depth):  16.2814
  - Abstractive Tendency (Δ):      0.0198
  - Average WSD for 'dense' prompts (Mean Spread): 9.2148
  - Average WSD for 'flat' prompts (Mean Spread):  9.2203
  - Focus Tendency (Φ):            0.0055

--- Interpretation ---
WLI (Weighted Layer Index) is the mean depth of processing.
**Δ (Abstractive Tendency)** = WLI_dense - WLI_flat. Higher Δ implies deeper processing for abstract tasks.
WSD (Weighted Std Dev) is the spread/focus of processing across layers.
**Φ (Focus Tendency)** = WSD_flat - WSD_dense. **Higher Φ implies flat tasks are more focused** (less spread) than dense tasks.
